# PK Awesome Agent Skills

A curated, machine-readable index of agent capabilities from Kingkillery skill repositories, with direct links to every SKILL.md.

![Skills](https://img.shields.io/badge/skills-1751-blue)
![Repos](https://img.shields.io/badge/repos-78-green)
![Format](https://img.shields.io/badge/format-Markdown%20%2B%20JSON-orange)

## At a Glance

- Source index: $HOME\.codex\kingkillery-agent-skill-repos.json
- Generated: 2026-05-09T15:47:56.1319902-06:00
- Total repositories: 78
- Total skills: 1751
- Refresh with: .\scripts\Update-PKAwesomeAgentSkills.ps1
- Rebuild README with: .\scripts\Generate-PKAwesomeReadme.ps1

## Files

- README.md: human-readable directory by category and by repository
- skills-flat.json: full flat list of links and metadata
- catalog.json: compressed index by repository
- scripts/Update-PKAwesomeAgentSkills.ps1: refresh JSON snapshots
- scripts/Generate-PKAwesomeReadme.ps1: regenerate this file

## Quick Search Strategy

1. Start in the category index when your ask is capability-based.
2. Open one or two SKILL.md files through the direct links.
3. If needed, follow to the owning repo for broader context.
